Title:  well, for often have I heard it on the field of battle, and in situations
Title:  which are frequent in a soldier's life. 'Tis the horrid shriek that a horse
Title:  will give in his agony; oftener drawn from him in pain, though sometimes in
Title:  terror. My charger is either a prey to the beasts of the forest, or he sees
Title:  his danger, without the power to avoid it. The sound might deceive me in the
Title:  cavern, but in the open air I know it too well to be wrong.
Title:  
Title:  The scout and his companions listened to this simple explanation with the
Title:  interest of men who imbibe new ideas, at the same time that they get rid of
Title:  old ones, which had proved disagreeable inmates. The two latter uttered
Title:  their usual expressive exclamation, hugh! as the truth first glanced upon
Title:  their minds, while the former, after a short, musing pause, took upon
Title:  himself to reply.
Title:  
Title:  I cannot deny your words, he said, for I am little skilled in horses, though
Title:  born where they abound. The wolves must be hovering above their heads on the
Title:  bank, and the timorsome creatures are calling on man for help, in the best
Title:  manner they are able. Uncas - he spoke in Delaware - Uncas, drop down in the
Title:  canoe, and whirl a brand among the pack; or fear may do what the wolves
Title:  can't get at to perform, and leave us without horses in the morning, when we
Title:  shall have so much need to journey swiftly!
Title:  
Title:  The young native had already descended to the water to comply, when a long
Title:  howl was raised on the edge of the river, and was borne swiftly off into the
Title:  depths of the forest, as though the beasts, of their own accord, were
Title:  abandoning their prey in sudden terror. Uncas, with instinctive quickness,
Title:  receded, and the three foresters held another of their low, earnest
Title:  conferences.
Title:  
Title:  We have been like hunters who have lost the points of the heavens, and from
Title:  whom the sun has been hid for days, said Hawkeye, turning away from his
Title:  companions; now we begin again to know the signs of our course, and the
Title:  paths are cleared from briers! Seat yourselves in the shade which the moon
Title:  throws from yonder beech - 'tis thicker than that of the pines - and let us
Title:  wait for that which the Lord may choose to send next. Let all your
Title:  conversation be in whispers; though it would be better, and, perhaps, in the
Title:  end, wiser, if each one held discourse with his own thoughts, for a time.
Title:  
Title:  The manner of the scout was seriously impressive, though no longer
Title:  distinguished by any signs of unmanly apprehension. It was evident that his
Title:  momentary weakness had vanished with the explanation of a mystery which his
Title:  own experience had not served to fathom; and though he now felt all the
Title:  realities of their actual condition, that he was prepared to meet them with
Title:  the energy of his hardy nature. This feeling seemed also common to the
Title:  natives, who placed themselves in positions which commanded a full view of
Title:  both shores, while their own persons were effectually concealed from
Title:  observation. In such circumstances, common prudence dictated that Heyward
Title:  and his companions should imitate a caution that proceeded from so
Title:  intelligent a source. The young man drew a pile of the sassafras from the
Title:  cave, and placing it in the chasm which separated the two caverns, it was
Title:  occupied by the sisters, who were thus protected by the rocks from any
Title:  missiles, while their anxiety was relieved by the assurance that no danger
Title:  could approach without a warning. Heyward himself was posted at hand, so
Title:  near that he might communicate with his companions without raising his voice
Title:  to a dangerous elevation; while David, in imitation of the woodsmen,
Title:  bestowed his person in such a manner among the fissures of the rocks, that
Title:  his ungainly limbs were no longer offensive to the eye.
Title:  
Title:  In this manner hours passed without further interruption. The moon reached
Title:  the zenith, and shed its mild light perpendicularly on the lovely sight of
Title:  the sisters slumbering peacefully in each other's arms. Duncan cast the wide
Title:  shawl of Cora before a spectacle he so much loved to contemplate, and then
Title:  suffered his own head to seek a pillow on the rock. David began to utter
Title:  sounds that would have shocked his delicate organs in more wakeful moments;
Title:  in short, all but Hawkeye and the Mohicans lost every idea of consciousness,
Title:  in uncontrollable drowsiness. But the watchfulness of these vigilant
Title:  protectors neither tired nor slumbered. Immovable as that rock, of which
Title:  each appeared to form a part, they lay, with their eyes roving, without
Title:  intermission, along the dark margin of trees, that bounded the adjacent
Title:  shores of the narrow stream. Not a sound escaped them; the most subtle
Title:  examination could not have told they breathed. It was evident that this
Title:  excess of caution proceeded from an experience that no subtlety on the part
Title:  of their enemies could deceive. It was, however, continued without any
Title:  apparent consequences, until the moon had set, and a pale streak above the
Title:  treetops, at the bend of the river a little below, announced the approach of
Title:  day.
Title:  
Title:  Then, for the first time, Hawkeye was seen to stir. He crawled along the
Title:  rock and shook Duncan from his heavy slumbers.
Title:  
Title:  Now is the time to journey, he whispered; awake the gentle ones, and be
Title:  ready to get into the canoe when I bring it to the landing-place.
Title:  
Title:  Have you had a quiet night? said Heyward; for myself, I believe sleep has
Title:  got the better of my vigilance.
Title:  
Title:  All is yet still as midnight. Be silent, but be quick.
Title:  
Title:  By this time Duncan was thoroughly awake, and he immediately lifted the
Title:  shawl from the sleeping females. The motion caused Cora to raise her hand as
Title:  if to repulse him, while Alice murmured, in her soft, gentle voice, No, no,
Title:  dear father, we were not deserted; Duncan was with us!
Title:  
Title:  Yes, sweet innocence, whispered the youth; Duncan is here, and while life
Title:  continues or danger remains, he will never quit thee. Cora! Alice! awake!
Title:  The hour has come to move!
Title:  
Title:  A loud shriek from the younger of the sisters, and the form of the other
Title:  standing upright before him, in bewildered horror, was the unexpected answer
Title:  he received.
Title:  
Title:  While the words were still on the lips of Heyward, there had arisen such a
Title:  tumult of yells and cries as served to drive the swift currents of his own
Title:  blood back from its bounding course into the fountains of his heart. It
Title:  seemed, for near a minute, as if the demons of hell had possessed themselves
Title:  of the air about them, and were venting their savage humors in barbarous
Title:  sounds. The cries came from no particular direction, though it was evident
Title:  they filled the woods, and, as the appalled listeners easily imagined, the
Title:  caverns of the falls, the rocks, the bed of the river, and the upper air.
Title:  David raised his tall person in the midst of the infernal din, with a hand
Title:  on either ear, exclaiming:
Title:  
Title:  Whence comes this discord! Has hell broke loose, that man should utter
Title:  sounds like these!
Title:  
Title:  The bright flashes and the quick reports of a dozen rifles, from the
Title:  opposite banks of the stream, followed this incautious exposure of his
Title:  person, and left the unfortunate singing master senseless on that rock where
Title:  he had been so long slumbering. The Mohicans boldly sent back the
Title:  intimidating yell of their enemies, who raised a shout of savage triumph at
Title:  the fall of Gamut. The flash of rifles was then quick and close between
Title:  them, but either party was too well skilled to leave even a limb exposed to
Title:  the hostile aim. Duncan listened with intense anxiety for the strokes of the
Title:  paddle, believing that flight was now their only refuge. The river glanced
Title:  by with its ordinary velocity, but the canoe was nowhere to be seen on its
Title:  dark waters. He had just fancied they were cruelly deserted by their scout,
Title:  as a stream of flame issued from the rock beneath them, and a fierce yell,
Title:  blended with a shriek of agony, announced that the messenger of death sent
Title:  from the fatal weapon of Hawkeye, had found a victim. At this slight repulse
Title:  the assailants instantly withdrew, and gradually the place became as still
Title:  as before the sudden tumult.
Title:  
Title:  Duncan seized the favorable moment to spring to the body of Gamut, which he
Title:  bore within the shelter of the narrow chasm that protected the sisters. In
Title:  another minute the whole party ws collected in this spot of comparative
Title:  safety.
Title:  
Title:  The poor fellow has saved his scalp, said Hawkeye, coolly passing his hand
Title:  over the head of David; but he is a proof that a man may be born with too
Title:  long a tongue! 'Twas downright madness to show six feet of flesh and blood,
Title:  on a naked rock, to the raging savages. I only wonder he has escaped with
Title:  life.
Title:  
Title:  Is he not dead? demanded Cora, in a voice whose husky tones showed how
Title:  powerfully natural horror struggled with her assumed firmness. Can we do
Title:  aught to assist the wretched man?
Title:  
Title:  No, no! the life is in his heart yet, and after he has slept awhile he will
Title:  come to himself, and be a wiser man for it, till the hour of his real time
Title:  shall come, returned Hawkeye, casting another oblique glance at the
Title:  insensible body, while he filled his charger with admirable nicety. Carry
Title:  him in, Uncas, and lay him on the sassafras. The longer his nap lasts the
Title:  better it will be for him, as I doubt whether he can find a proper cover for
Title:  such a shape on these rocks; and singing won't do any good with the
Title:  Iroquois.
Title:  
Title:  You believe, then, the attack will be renewed? asked Heyward.
Title:  
Title:  Do I expect a hungry wolf will satisfy his craving with a mouthful! They
Title:  have lost a man, and 'tis their fashion, when they meet a loss, and fail in
Title:  the surprise, to fall back; but we shall have them on again, with new
Title:  expedients to circumvent us, and master our scalps. Our main hope, he
Title:  continued, raising his rugged countenance, across which a shade of anxiety
Title:  just then passed like a darkening cloud, will be to keep the rock until
Title:  Munro can send a party to our help! God send it may be soon and under a
Title:  leader that knows the Indian customs!
Title:  
Title:  You hear our probable fortunes, Cora, said Duncan, and you know we have
Title:  everything to hope from the anxiety and experience of your father. Come,
Title:  then, with Alice, into this cavern, where you, at least, will be safe from
Title:  the murderous rifles of our enemies, and where you may bestow a care suited
Title:  to your gentle natures on our unfortunate comrade.
Title:  
Title:  The sisters followed him into the outer cave, where David was beginning, by
Title:  his sighs, to give symptoms of returning consciousness, and then commending
Title:  the wounded man to their attention, he immediately prepared to leave them.
Title:  
Title:  Duncan! said the tremulous voice of Cora, when he had reached the mouth of
Title:  the cavern. He turned and beheld the speaker, whose color had changed to a
Title:  deadly paleness, and whose lips quivered, gazing after him, with an
Title:  expression of interest which immediately recalled him to her side. Remember,
Title:  Duncan, how necessary your safety is to our own - how you bear a father's
Title:  sacred trust - how much depends on your discretion and care - in short, she
Title:  added, while the telltale blood stole over her features, crimsoning her very
Title:  temples, how very deservedly dear you are to all of the name of Munro.
Title:  
Title:  If anything could add to my own base love of life, said Heyward, suffering
Title:  his unconscious eyes to wander to the youthful form of the silent Alice, it
Title:  would be so kind an assurance. As major of the Sixtieth, our honest host
Title:  will tell you I must take my share of the fray; but our task will be easy;
Title:  it is merely to keep these blood-hounds at bay for a few hours.
Title:  
Title:  Without waiting for a reply, he tore himself from the presence of the
Title:  sisters, and joined the scout and his companions, who stil lay within the
Title:  protection of the little chasm between the two caves.
Title:  
Title:  I tell you, Uncas, said the former, as Heyward joined them, you are wasteful
Title:  of your powder, and the kick of the rifle disconcerts your aim! Little
Title:  powder, light lead, and a long arm, seldom fail of bringing the death
Title:  screech from a Mingo! At least, such has been my experience with the
Title:  creatur's. Come, friends: let us to our covers, for no man can tell when or
Title:  where a Maqua1 will strike his blow.
Title:  
Title:  The Indians silently repaired to their appointed stations, which were
Title:  fissures in the rocks, whence they could command the approaches to the foot
Title:  of the falls. In the center of the little island, a few short and stunted
Title:  pines had found root, forming a thicket, into which Hawkeye darted with the
Title:  swiftness of a deer, followed by the active Duncan. Here they secured
Title:  themselves, as well as circumstances would permit, among the shrubs and
Title:  fragments of stone that were scattered about the place. Above them was a
Title:  bare, rounded rock, on each side of which the water played its gambols, and
Title:  plunged into the abysses beneath, in the manner already described. As the
Title:  day had now dawned, the opposite shores no longer presented a confused
Title:  outline, but they were able to look into the woods, and distinguish objects
Title:  beneath a canopy of gloomy pines.
Title:  
Title:  A long and anxious watch succeeded, but without any further evidences of a
Title:  renewed attack; and Duncan began to hope that their fire had proved more
Title:  fatal than was supposed, and that their enemies had been effectually
Title:  repulsed. When he ventured to utter this impression to his companions, it
Title:  was met by Hawkeye with an incredulous shake of the head.
Title:  
Title:  You know not the nature of a Maqua, if you think he is so easily beaten back
Title:  without a scalp! he answered. If there was one of the imps yelling this
Title:  morning, there were forty! and they know our number and quality too well to
Title:  give up the chase so soon. Hist! look into the water above, just where it
Title:  breaks over the rocks. I am no mortal, if the risky devils haven't swam down
Title:  upon the very pitch, and, as bad luck would have it, they have hit the head
Title:  of the island. Hist! man, keep close! or the hair will be off your crown in
Title:  the turning of a knife!
Title:  
Title:  Heyward lifted his head from the cover, and beheld what he justly considered
Title:  a prodigy of rashness and skill. The river had worn away the edge of the
Title:  soft rock in such a manner as to render its first pitch less abrupt and
Title:  perpendicular than is usual at waterfalls. With no other guide than the
Title:  ripple of the stream where it met the head of the island, a party of their
Title:  insatiable foes had ventured into the current, and swam down upon this
Title:  point, knowing the ready access it would give, if successful, to their
Title:  intended victims.
Title:  
Title:  As Hawkeye ceased speaking, four human heads could be seen peering above a
Title:  few logs of drift-wood that had lodged on these naked rocks, and which had
Title:  probably suggested the idea of the practicability of the hazardous
Title:  undertaking. At the next moment, a fifth form was seen floating over the
Title:  green edge of the fall, a little from the line of the island. The savage
Title:  struggled powerfully to gain the point of safety, and, favored by the
Title:  glancing water, he was already stretching forth an arm to meet the grasp of
Title:  his companions, when he shot away again with the shirling current, appeared
Title:  to rise into the air, with uplifted arms and starting eyeballs, and fell,
Title:  with a sudden plunge, into that deep and yawning abyss over which he
Title:  hovered. A single, wild, despairing shriek rose from the cavern, and all was
Title:  hushed again as the grave.
Title:  
Title:  The first generous impulse of Duncan was to rush to the rescue of the
Title:  hapless wretch; but he felt himself bound to the spot by the iron grasp of
Title:  the immovable scout.
Title:  
Title:  Would ye bring certain death upon us, by telling the Mingoes where we lie?
Title:  demanded Hawkeye, sternly; 'Tis a charge of powder saved, and ammunition is
Title:  as precious now as breath to a worried deer! Freshen the priming of your
Title:  pistols - the midst of the falls is apt to dampen the brimstone - and stand
Title:  firm for a close struggle, while I fire on their rush.
Title:  
Title:  He placed a finger in his mouth, and drew a long, shrill whistle, which was
Title:  answered from the rocks that were guarded by the Mohicans. Duncan caught
Title:  glimpses of heads above the scattered drift-wood, as this signal rose on the
Title:  air, but they disappeared again as suddenly as they had glanced upon his
Title:  sight. A low, rustling sound next drew his attention behind him, and turning
Title:  his head, he beheld Uncas within a few feet, creeping to his side. Hawkeye
Title:  spoke to him in Delaware, when the young chief took his position with
Title:  singular caution and undisturbed coolness. To Heyward this was a moment of
Title:  feverish and impatient suspense; though the scout saw fit to select it as a
Title:  fit occasion to read a lecture to his more youthful associates on the art of
Title:  using firearms with discretion.
Title:  
Title:  Of all we'pons, he commenced, the long barreled, true-grooved, soft-metaled
Title:  rifle is the most dangerous in skillful hands, though it wants a strong arm,
Title:  a quick eye, and great judgment in charging, to put forth all its beauties.
Title:  The gunsmiths can have but little insight into their trade when they make
Title:  their fowling-pieces and short horsemen's - -
Title:  
Title:  He was interrupted by the low but expressive hugh of Uncas.
Title:  
Title:  I see them, boy, I see them! continued Hawkeye; they are gathering for the
Title:  rush, or they would keep their dingy backs below the logs. Well, let them,
Title:  he added, examining his flint; the leading man certainly comes on to his
Title:  death, though it should be Montcalm himself!
Title:  
Title:  At that moment the woods were filled with another burst of cries, and at the
Title:  signal four savages sprang from the cover of the driftwood. Heyward felt a
Title:  burning desire to rush forward to meet them, so intense was the delirious
Title:  anxiety of the moment; but he was restrained by the deliberate examples of
Title:  the scout and Uncas.
Title:  
Title:  When their foes, who had leaped over the black rocks that divided them, with
Title:  long bounds, uttering the wildest yells, were within a few rods, the rifle
Title:  of Hawkeye slowly rose among the shrubs, and poured out its fatal contents.
Title:  The foremost Indian bounded like a striken deer, and fell headlong among the
Title:  clefts of the island.
Title:  
Title:  Now, Uncas! cried the scout, drawing his long knife, while his quick eyes
Title:  began to flash with ardor, take the last of the screeching imps; of the
Title:  other two we are sartain!
Title:  
Title:  He was obeyed; and but two enemies remained to be overcome. Heyward had
Title:  given one of his pistols to Hawkeye, and together they rushed down a little
Title:  declivity toward their foes; they discharged their weapons at the same
Title:  instant, and equally without success.
Title:  
Title:  I know'd it! and I said it! muttered the scout, whirling the despised little
Title:  implement over the falls with bitter disdain. Come on, ye bloody minded
Title:  hell-hounds! ye meet a man without a cross!
Title:  
Title:  The words were barely uttered, when he encountered a savage of gigantic
Title:  stature, of the fiercest mien. At the same moment, Duncan found himself
Title:  engaged with the other, in a similar contest of hand to hand. With ready
Title:  skill, Hawkeye and his antagonist each grasped that uplifted arm of the
Title:  other which held the dangerous knife. For near a minute they stood looking
Title:  one another in the eye, and gradually exerting the power of their muscles
Title:  for the mastery.
Title:  
Title:  At length, the toughened sinews of the white man prevailed over the less
Title:  practiced limbs of the native. The arm of the latter slowly gave way before
Title:  the increasing force of the scout, who, suddenly wresting his armed hand
Title:  from the grasp of the foe, drove the sharp weapon through his naked bosom to
Title:  the heart. In the meantime, Heyward had been pressed in a more deadly
Title:  struggle. His slight sword was snapped in the first encounter. As he was
Title:  destitute of any other means of defense, his safety now depended entirely on
Title:  bodily strength and resolution. Though deficient in neither of these
Title:  qualities, he had met an enemy every way his equal. Happily, he soon
Title:  succeeded in disarming his adversary, whose knife fell on the rock at their
Title:  feet; and from this moment it became a fierce struggle who should cast the
Title:  other over the dizzy height into a neighboring cavern of the falls. Every
Title:  successive struggle brought them nearer to the verge, where Duncan perceived
Title:  the final and conquering effort must be made. Each of the combatants threw
Title:  all his energies into that effort, and the result was, that both tottered on
Title:  the brink of the precipice. Heyward felt the grasp of the other at his
Title:  throat, and saw the grim smile the savage gave, under the revengeful hope
Title:  that he hurried his enemy to a fate similar to his own, as he felt his body
Title:  slowly yielding to a resistless power, and the young man experienced the
Title:  passing agony of such a moment in all its horrors. At that instant of
Title:  extreme danger, a dark hand and glancing knife appeared before him; the
Title:  Indian released his hold, as the blood flowed freely from around the severed
Title:  tendons of the wrist; and while Duncan was drawn backward by the saving hand
Title:  of Uncas, his charmed eyes still were riveted on the fierce and disappointed
Title:  countenance of his foe, who fell sullenly and disappointed down the
Title:  irrecoverable precipice.
Title:  
Title:  To cover! to cover! cried Hawkeye, who just then had despatched the enemy;
Title:  to cover, for your lives! the work is but half ended!
Title:  
Title:  The young Mohican gave a shout of triumph, and followed by Duncan, he glided
Title:  up the acclivity they had descended to the combat, and sought the friendly
Title:  shelter of the rocks and shrubs.
Title:  
Title:  -----------------------
Title:  
Title:  1 Mingo was the Delaware term of the Five Nations. Maquas was the name given
Title:  them by the Dutch. The French, from their first intercourse with them,
Title:  called them Iroquois.
Title:  
Title:                 ----------------------------------------------
Title:  
Title:  Chapter 8
Title:  
Title:       They linger yet,
Title:       Avengers of their native land.
Title:  
Title:                                                                    GRAY
Title:  
Title:  The warning call of the scout was not uttered without occasion. During the
Title:  occurrence of the deadly encounter just related, the roar of the falls was
Title:  unbroken by any human sound whatever. It would seem that interest in the
Title:  result had kept the natives on the opposite shores in breathless suspense,
Title:  while the quick evolutions and swift changes in the positions of the
Title:  combatants effectually prevented a fire that might prove dangerous alike to
Title:  friend and enemy. But the moment the struggle was decided, a yell arose as
Title:  fierce and savage as wild and revengeful passions could throw into the air.
Title:  It was followed by the swift flashes of the rifles, which sent their leaden
Title:  messengers across the rock in volleys, as though the assailants would pour
Title:  out their impotent fury on the insensible scene of the fatal contest.
Title:  
Title:  A steady, though deliberate return was made from the rifle of Chingachgook,
Title:  who had maintained his post throughout the fray with unmoved resolution.
Title:  When the triumphant shout of Uncas was borne to his ears, the gratified
Title:  father raised his voice in a single responsive cry, after which his busy
Title:  piece alone proved that he still guarded his pass with unwearied diligence.
Title:  In this manner many minutes flew by with the swiftness of thought; the
Title:  rifles of the assailants speaking, at times, in rattling volleys, and at
Title:  others in occasional, scattering shots. Though the rock, the trees, and the
Title:  shrubs, were cut and torn in a hundred places around the besieged, their
Title:  cover was so close, and so rigidly maintained, that, as yet, David had been
Title:  the only sufferer in their little band.
Title:  
Title:  Let them burn their powder, said the deliberate scout, while bullet after
Title:  bullet whizzed by the place where he securely lay; there will be a fine
Title:  gathering of lead when it is over, and I fancy the imps will tire of the
Title:  sport afore these old stones cry out for mercy! Uncas, boy, you waste the
Title:  kernels by overcharging; and a kicking rifle never carries a true bullet. I
Title:  told you to take that loping miscreant under the line of white point; now,
Title:  if your bullet went a hair's breadth it went two inches above it. The life
Title:  lies low in a Mingo, and humanity teaches us to make a quick end to the
Title:  sarpents.
Title:  
Title:  A quiet smile lighted the haughty features of the young Mohican, betraying
Title:  his knowledge of the English language as well as of the other's meaning; but
Title:  he suffered it to pass away without vindication of reply.
Title:  
Title:  I cannot permit you to accuse Uncas of want of judgment or of skill, said
Title:  Duncan; he saved my life in the coolest and readiest manner, and he has made
Title:  a friend who never will require to be reminded of the debt he owes.
Title:  
Title:  Uncas partly raised his body, and offered his hand to the grasp of Heyward.
Title:  During this act of friendship, the two young men exchanged looks of
Title:  intelligence which caused Duncan to forget the character and condition of
Title:  his wild associate. In the meanwhile, Hawkeye, who looked on this burst of
Title:  youthful feeling with a cool but kind regard made the following reply:
Title:  
Title:  Life is an obligation which friends often owe each other in the wilderness.
Title:  I dare say I may have served Uncas some such turn myself before now; and I
Title:  very well remember that he has stood between me and death five different
Title:  times; three times from the Mingoes, once in crossing Horican, and - -
Title:  
Title:  That bullet was better aimed than common! exclaimed Duncan, involuntarily
Title:  shrinking from a shot which struck the rock at his side with a smart
Title:  rebound.
Title:  
Title:  Hawkeye laid his hand on the shapeless metal, and shook his head, as he
Title:  examined it, saying, Falling lead is never flattened, had it come from the
Title:  clouds this might have happened.
Title:  
Title:  But the rifle of Uncas was deliberately raised toward the heavens, directing
Title:  the eyes of his companions to a point, where the mystery was immediately
Title:  explained. A ragged oak grew on the right bank of the river, nearly opposite
Title:  to their position, which, seeking the freedom of the open space, had
Title:  inclined so far forward that its upper branches overhung that arm of the
Title:  stream which flowed nearest to its own shore. Among the topmost leaves,
Title:  which scantily concealed the gnarled and stunted limbs, a savage was
Title:  nestled, partly concealed by the trunk of the tree, and partly exposed, as
Title:  though looking down upon them to ascertain the effect produced by his
Title:  treacherous aim.
Title:  
Title:  These devils will scale heaven to circumvent us to our ruin, said Hawkeye;
Title:  keep him in play, boy, until I can bring killdeer to bear, when we will try
Title:  his metal on each side of the tree at once.
Title:  
Title:  Uncas delayed his fire until the scout uttered the word. The rifles flashed,
Title:  the leaves and bark of the oak flew into the air, and were scattered by the
Title:  wind, but the Indian answered their assault by a taunting laugh, sending
Title:  down upon them another bullet in return, that struck the cap of Hawkeye from
Title:  his head. Once more the savage yells burst out of the woods, and the leaden
Title:  hail whistled above the heads of the besieged, as if to confine them to a
Title:  place where they might become easy victims to the enterprise of the warrior
Title:  who had mounted the tree.
Title:  
Title:  This must be looked to, said the scout, glancing about him with an anxious
Title:  eye. Uncas, call up your father; we have need of all our we'pons to bring
Title:  the cunning varmint from his roost.
Title:  
Title:  The signal was instantly given; and, before Hawkeye had reloaded his rifle,
Title:  they were joined by Chingachgook. When his son pointed out to the
Title:  experienced warrior the situation of their dangerous enemy, the usual
Title:  exclamatory hugh burst from his lips; after which, no further expression of
Title:  surprise or alarm was suffered to escape him. Hawkeye and the Mohicans
Title:  conversed earnestly together in Delaware for a few moments, when each
Title:  quietly took his post, in order to execute the plan they had speedily
Title:  devised.
Title:  
Title:  The warrior in the oak had maintained a quick, though ineffectual fire, from
Title:  the moment of his discovery. But his aim was interrupted by the vigilance of
Title:  his enemies, whose rifles instantaneously bore on any part of his person
Title:  that was left exposed. Still his bullets fell in the center of the crouching
Title:  party. The clothes of Heyward, which rendered him peculiarly conspicuous,
Title:  were repeatedly cut, and once blood was drawn from a slight wound in his
Title:  arm.
Title:  
Title:  At length, emboldened by the long and patient watchfulness of his enemies,
Title:  the Huron attempted a better and more fatal aim. The quick eyes of the
Title:  Mohicans caught the dark line of his lower limbs incautiously exposed
Title:  through the thin foliage, a few inches from the trunk of the tree. Their
Title:  rifles made a common report, when, sinking on his wounded limb, part of the
Title:  body of the savage came into view. Swift as thought, Hawkeye seized the
Title:  advantage, and discharged his fatal weapon into the top of the oak. The
Title:  leaves were unusually agitated; the dangerous rifle fell from its commanding
Title:  elevation, and after a few moments of vain struggling, the form of the
Title:  savage was seen swinging in the wind, while he still grasped a ragged and
Title:  naked branch of the tree with hands clenched in desperation.
Title:  
Title:  Give him, in pity, give him the contents of another rifle, cried Duncan,
Title:  turning away his eyes in horror from the spectacle of a fellow creature in
Title:  such awful jeopardy.
Title:  
Title:  Not a karnel! exclaimed the obdurate Hawkeye; his death is certain, and we
Title:  have no powder to spare, for Indian fights sometimes last for days; tis
Title:  their scalps or ours! and God, who made us, has put into our natures the
Title:  craving to keep the skin on the head.
Title:  
Title:  Against this stern and unyielding morality, supported as it was by such
Title:  visible policy, there was no appeal. From that moment the yells in the
Title:  forest once more ceased, the fire was suffered to decline, and all eyes,
Title:  those of friends as well as enemies, became fixed on the hopeless condition
Title:  of the wretch who was dangling between heaven and earth. The body yielded to
Title:  the currents of air, and though no murmur or groan escaped the victim, there
Title:  were instants when he grimly faced his foes, and the anguish of cold despair
Title:  might be traced, through the intervening distance, in possession of his
Title:  swarthy lineaments. Three several times the scout raised his piece in mercy,
Title:  and as often, prudence getting the better of his intention, it was again
Title:  silently lowered. At length one hand of the Huron lost its hold, and dropped
Title:  exhausted to his side. A desperate and fruitless struggle to recover the
Title:  branch succeeded, and then the savage was seen for a fleeting instant,
Title:  grasping wildly at the empty air. The lightning is not quicker than was the
Title:  flame from the rifle of Hawkeye; the limbs of the victim trembled and
Title:  contracted, the head fell to the bosom, and the body parted the foaming
Title:  waters like lead, when the element closed above it, in its ceaseless
Title:  velocity, and every vestige of the unhappy Huron was lost forever.
Title:  
Title:  No shout of triumph succeeded this important advantage, but even the
Title:  Mohicans gazed at each other in silent horror. A single yell burst from the
Title:  woods, and all was again still. Hawkeye, who alone appeared to reason on the
Title:  occasion, shook his head at his own momentary weakness, even uttering his
Title:  self-disapprobation aloud.
Title:  
Title:  'Twas the last charge in my horn and the last bullet in my pouch, and 'twas
Title:  the act of a boy! he said; what mattered it whether he struck the rock
Title:  living or dead! feeling would soon be over. Uncas, lad, go down to the
Title:  canoe, and bring up the big horn; it is all the powder we have left, and we
Title:  shall need it to the last grain, or I am ignorant of the Mingo nature.
Title:  
Title:  The young Mohican complied, leaving the scout turning over the useless
Title:  contents of his pouch, and shaking the empty horn with renewed discontent.
Title:  From this unsatisfactory examination, however, he was soon called by a loud
Title:  and piercing exclamation from Uncas, that sounded, even to the unpracticed
Title:  ears of Duncan, as the signal of some new and unexpected calamity. Every
Title:  thought filled with apprehension for the previous treasure he had concealed
Title:  in the cavern, the young man started to his feet, totally regardless of the
Title:  hazard he incurred by such an exposure. As if actuated by a common impulse,
Title:  his movement was imitated by his companions, and, together they rushed down
Title:  the pass to the friendly chasm, with a rapidity that rendered the scattering
Title:  fire of their enemies perfectly harmless. The unwonted cry had brought the
Title:  sisters, together with the wounded David, from their place of refuge; and
Title:  the whole party, at a single glance, was made acquainted with the nature of
Title:  the disaster that had disturbed even the practiced stoicism of their
Title:  youthful Indian protector.
Title:  
Title:  At a short distance from the rock, their little bark was to be seen floating
Title:  across the eddy, toward the swift current of the river, in a manner which
Title:  proved that its course was directed by some hidden agent. The instant this
Title:  unwelcome sight caught the eye of the scout, his rifle was leveled as by
Title:  instinct, but the barrel gave no answer to the bright sparks of the flint.
Title:  
Title:  'Tis too late, 'tis too late! Hawkeye exclaimed, dropping the useless piece
Title:  in bitter disappointment; the miscreant has struck the rapid; and had we
Title:  powder, it could hardly send the lead swifter than he now goes!
Title:  
Title:  The adventurous Huron raised his head above the shelter of the canoe, and,
Title:  while it glided swiftly down the stream, he waved his hand, and gave forth
Title:  the shout, which was the known signal of success. His cry was answered by a
Title:  yell and a laugh from the woods, as tauntingly exulting as if fifty demons
Title:  were uttering their blasphemies at the fall of some Christian soul.
Title:  
Title:  Well may you laugh, ye children of the devil! said the scout, seating
Title:  himself on a projection of the rock, and suffering his gun to fall neglected
Title:  at his feet, for the three quickest and truest rifles in these woods are no
Title:  better than so many stalks of mullein, or the last year's horns of a buck!
Title:  
Title:  What is to be done? demanded Duncan, losing the first feeling of
Title:  disappointment in a more manly desire for exertion; what will become of us?
Title:  
Title:  Hawkeye made no other reply than by passing his finger around the crown of
Title:  his head, in a manner so significant, that none who witnessed the action
Title:  could mistake its meaning.
Title:  
Title:  Surely, surely, our case is not so desperate! exclaimed the youth; the
Title:  Hurons are not here; we may make good the caverns, we may oppose their
Title:  landing.
Title:  
Title:  With what? coolly demanded the scout. The arrows of Uncas, or such tears as
Title:  women shed! No, no; you are young, and rich, and have friends, and at such
Title:  an age I know it is hard to die! But, glancing his eyes at the Mohicans, let
Title:  us remember we are men without a cross, and let us teach these natives of
Title:  the forest that white blood can run as freely as red, when the appointed
Title:  hour is come.
Title:  
Title:  Duncan turned quickly in the direction indicated by the other's eyes, and
Title:  read a confirmation of his worst apprehensions in the conduct of the
Title:  Indians. Chingachgook, placing himself in a dignified posture on another
Title:  fragment of the rock, had already laid aside his knife and tomahawk, and was
Title:  in the act of taking the eagle's plume from his head, and smoothing the
Title:  solitary tuft of hair in readiness to perform its last and revolting office.
Title:  His countenance was composed, though thoughtful, while his dark, gleaming
Title:  eyes were gradually losing the fierceness of the combat in an expression
Title:  better suited to the change he expected momentarily to undergo.
Title:  
Title:  Our case is not, cannot be so hopeless! said Duncan; even at this very
Title:  moment succor may be at hand. I see no enemies! They have sickened of a
Title:  struggle in which they risk so much with so little prospect of gain!
Title:  
Title:  It may be a minute, or it may be an hour, afore the wily sarpents steal upon
Title:  us, and it is quite in natur' for them to be lying within hearing at this
Title:  very moment, said Hawkeye; but come they will, and in such a fashion as will
Title:  leave us nothing to hope! Chingachgook - he spoke in Delaware - my brother,
Title:  we have fought our last battle together, and the Maquas will triumph in the
Title:  death of the sage man of the Mohicans, and of the pale face, whose eyes can
Title:  make night as day, and level the clouds to the mists of the springs!
Title:  
Title:  Let the Mingo women go weep over the slain! returned the Indian, with
Title:  characteristic pride and unmoved firmness; the Great Snake of the Mohicans
Title:  has coiled himself in their wigwams, and has poisoned their triumph with the
Title:  wailings of children, whose fathers have not returned! Eleven warriors lie
Title:  hid form the graves of their tribes since the snows have melted, and none
Title:  will tell where to find them when the tongue of Chingachgook shall be
Title:  silent! Let them draw the sharpest knife, and whirl the swiftest tomahawk,
Title:  for their bitterest enemy is in their hands. Uncas, topmost branch of a
Title:  noble trunk, call on the cowards to hasten, or their hearts will soften, and
Title:  they will change to women!
Title:  
Title:  They look among the fishes for their dead! returned the low, soft voice of
Title:  the youthful chieftain; the Hurons float with the slimy eels! They drop from
Title:  the oaks like fruit that is ready to be eaten! and the Delawares laugh!
Title:  
Title:  Ay, ay, muttered the scout, who had listened to this peculiar burst of the
Title:  natives with deep attention; they have warmed their Indian feelings, and
Title:  they'll soon provoke the Maquas to give them a speedy end. As for me, who am
Title:  of the whole blood of the whites, it is befitting that I should die as
Title:  becomes my color, with no words of scoffing in my mouth, and without
Title:  bitterness at the heart!
Title:  
Title:  Why die at all! said Cora, advancing from the place where natural horror
Title:  had, until this moment, held her riveted to the rock; the path is open on
Title:  every side; fly, then, to the woods, and call on God for succor. Go, brave
Title:  men, we owe you too much already; let us no longer involve you in our
Title:  hapless fortunes!
Title:  
Title:  You but little know the craft of the Iroquois, lady, if you judge they have
Title:  left the path open to the woods! returned Hawkeye, who, however, immediately
Title:  added in his simplicity, the down stream current, it is certain, might soon
Title:  sweep us beyond the reach of their rifles or the sound of their voices.
Title:  
Title:  Then try the river. Why linger to add to the number of the victims of our
Title:  merciless enemies?
Title:  
Title:  Why, repeated the scout, looking about him proudly; because it is better for
Title:  a man to die at peace with himself than to live haunted by an evil
Title:  conscience! What answer could we give Munro, when he asked us where and how
Title:  we left his children?
Title:  
Title:  Go to him, and say that you left them with a message to hasten to their aid,
Title:  returned Cora, advancing nigher to the scout in her generous ardor; that the
Title:  Hurons bear them into the northern wilds, but that by vigilance and speed
Title:  they may yet be rescued; and if, after all, it should please heaven that his
Title:  assistance come too late, bear to him, she continued, her voice gradually
Title:  lowering, until it seemed nearly choked, the love, the blessings, the final
Title:  prayers of his daughters, and bid him not mourn their early fate, but to
Title:  look forward with humble confidence to the Christian's goal to meet his
Title:  children.
Title:  
Title:  The hard, weather-beaten features of the scout began to work, and when she
Title:  had ended, he dropped his chin to his hand, like a man musing profoundly on
Title:  the nature of the proposal.
Title:  
Title:  There is reason in her words! at length broke from his compressed and
Title:  trembling lips; ay, and they bear the spirit of Christianity; what might be
Title:  right and proper in a red-skin, may be sinful in a man who has not even a
Title:  cross in blood to plead for his ignorance. Chingachgook! Uncas! hear you the
Title:  talk of the dark-eyed woman?
Title:  
Title:  He now spoke in Delaware to his companions, and his address, though calm and
Title:  deliberate, seemed very decided. The elder Mohican heard with deep gravity,
Title:  and appeared to ponder on his words, as though he felt the importance of
Title:  their import. After a moment of hesitation, he waved his hand in assent, and
Title:  uttered the English word Good! with the peculiar emphasis of his people.
Title:  Then, replacing his knife and tomahawk in his girdle, the warrior moved
Title:  silently to the edge of the rock which was most concealed from the banks of
Title:  the river. Here he paused a moment, pointed significantly to the woods
Title:  below, and saying a few words in his own language, as if indicating his
Title:  intended route, he dropped into the water, and sank from before the eyes of
Title:  the witnesses of his movements.
Title:  
Title:  The scout delayed his departure to speak to the generous girl, whose
Title:  breathing became lighter as she saw the success of her remonstrance.
Title:  
Title:  Wisdom is sometimes given to the young, as well as to the old, he said; and
Title:  what you have spoken is wise, not to call it by a better word. If you are
Title:  led into the woods, that is such of you as may be spared for awhile, break
Title:  the twigs on the bushes as you pass, and make the marks of your trail as
Title:  broad as you can, when, if mortal eyes can see them, depend on having a
Title:  friend who will follow to the ends of the 'arth afore he desarts you.
Title:  
Title:  He gave Cora an affectionate shake of the hand, lifted his rifle, and after
Title:  regarding it a moment with melancholy solicitude, laid it carefully aside,
Title:  and descended to the place where Chingachgook had just disappeared. For an
Title:  instant he hung suspended by the rock, and looking about him, with a
Title:  countenance of peculiar care, he added bitterly, Had the powder held out,
Title:  this disgrace could never have befallen! then, loosening his hold, the water
Title:  closed above his head, and he also became lost to view.
Title:  
Title:  All eyes now were turned on Uncas, who stood leaning against the ragged
Title:  rock, in immovable composure. After waiting a short time, Cora pointed down
Title:  the river, and said:
Title:  
Title:  Your friends have not been seen, and are now, most probably, in safety. Is
Title:  it not time for you to follow?
Title:  
Title:  Uncas will stay, the young Mohican calmly answered in English.
Title:  
Title:  To increase the horror of our capture, and to diminish the chances of our
Title:  release! Go, generous young man, Cora continued, lowering her eyes under the
Title:  gaze of the Mohican, and perhaps, with an intuitive consciousness of her
Title:  power; go to my father, as I have said, and be the most confidential of my
Title:  messengers. Tell him to trust you with the means to buy the freedom of his
Title:  daughters. Go!'tis my wish, 'tis my prayer, that you will go!
Title:  
Title:  The settled, calm look of the young chief changed to an expression of gloom,
Title:  but he no longer hesitated. With a noiseless step he crossed the rock, and
Title:  dropped into the troubled stream. Hardly a breath was drawn by those he left
Title:  behind, until they caught a glimpse of his head emerging for air, far down
Title:  the current, when he again sank, and was seen no more.
Title:  
Title:  These sudden and apparently successful experiments had all taken place in a
Title:  few minutes of that time which had now become so precious. After a last look
Title:  at Uncas, Cora turne,d and with a quivering lip, addressed herself to
Title:  Heyward:
Title:  
Title:  I have heard of your boasted skill in the water, too, Duncan, she said;
Title:  follow, then, the wise example set you by these simple and faithful beings.
Title:  
Title:  Is such the faith that Cora Munro would exact from her protector? said the
Title:  young man, smiling mournfully, but with bitterness.
Title:  
Title:  This is not a time for idle subtleties and false opinions, she answered; but
Title:  a moment when every duty should be equally considered. To us you can be of
Title:  no further service here, but your precious life may be saved for other and
Title:  nearer friends.
Title:  
Title:  He made no reply, though his eye fell wistfully on the beautiful form of
Title:  Alice, who was clinging to his arm with the dependency of an infant.
Title:  
Title:  Consider, continued Cora, after a pause, during which she seemed to struggle
Title:  with a pang even more acute than any that her fears had excited, that the
Title:  worst to us can be but death; a tribute that all must pay at the good time
Title:  of God's appointment.
Title:  
Title:  There are evils worse than death, said Duncan, speaking hoarsely, and as if
Title:  fretful at her importunity, but which the presence of one who would die in
Title:  your behalf may avert.
Title:  
Title:  Cora ceased her entreaties; and veiling her face in her shawl, drew the
Title:  nearly insensible Alice after her into the deepest recess of the inner
Title:  cavern.
Title:  
Title:                 ----------------------------------------------
Title:  
Title:  Chapter 9
Title:  
Title:       Be gay securely;
Title:       Dispel, my fair, with smiles, the tim'rous clouds,
Title:       That hang on thy clear brow.
Title:  
Title:                                                      DEATH OF AGRIPPINA
Title:  
Title:  The sudden and almost magical change, from the stirring incidents of the
Title:  combat to the stillness that now reigned around him, acted on the heated
Title:  imagination of Heyward like some exciting dream. While all the images and
Title:  events he had witnessed remained deeply impressed on his memory, he felt a
Title:  difficulty in persuading him of their truth. Still ignorant of the fate of
Title:  those who had trusted to the aid of the swift current, he at first listened
Title:  intently to any signal or sounds of alarm, which might announce the good or
Title:  evil fortune of their hazardous undertaking. His attention was, however,
Title:  bestowed in vain; for with the disappearance of Uncas, every sign of the
Title:  adventurers had been lost, leaving him in total uncertainty of their fate.
Title:  
Title:  In a moment of such painful doubt, Duncan did not hesitate to look around
Title:  him, without consulting that protection from the rocks which just before had
Title:  been so necessary to his safety. Every effort, however, to detect the least
Title:  evidence of the approach of their hidden enemies was as fruitless as the
Title:  inquiry after his late companions. The wooded banks of the river seemed
Title:  again deserted by everything possessing animal life. The uproar which had so
Title:  lately echoed through the vaults of the forest was gone, leaving the rush of
Title:  the waters to swell and sink on the currents of the air, in the unmingled
Title:  sweetness of nature. A fish-hawk, which, secure on the topmost branches of a
Title:  dead pine, had been a distant spectator of the fray, now swooped form his
Title:  high and ragged perch, and soared, in wide sweeps, above his prey; while a
Title:  jay, whose noisy voice had been stilled by the hoarser cries of the savages,
Title:  ventured again to open his discordant throat, as though once more in
Title:  undisturbed possession of his wild domains. Duncan caught from these natural
Title:  accompaniments of the solitary scene a glimmering of hope; and he began to
Title:  rally his faculties to renewed exertions, with something like a reviving
Title:  confidence of success.
Title:  
Title:  The Hurons are not to be seen, he said, addressing David, who had by no
Title:  means recovered from the effects of the stunning blow he had received; let
Title:  us conceal ourselves in the cavern, and trust the rest to Providence.
Title:  
Title:  I remember to have united with two comely maidens, in lifting up our voices
Title:  in praise and thanksgiving, returned the bewildered singing-master; since
Title:  which time I have been visited by a heavy judgment for my sins. I have been
Title:  mocked with the likensss of sleep, while sounds of discord have rent my
Title:  ears, such as might manifest the fullness of time, and that nature had
Title:  forgotten her harmony.
Title:  
Title:  Poor fellow! thine own period was, in truth, near its accomplishment! But
Title:  arouse, and come with me; I will lead you where all other sounds but those
Title:  of your own psalmody shall be excluded.
Title:  
Title:  There is melody in the fall of the cataract, and the rushing of many waters
Title:  is sweet to the senses! said David, pressing his hand confusedly on his
Title:  brow. Is not the air yet filled with shrieks and cries, as though the
Title:  departed spirits of the damned - -
Title:  
Title:  Not now, not now, interrupted the impatient Heyward, they have ceased, and
Title:  they who raised them, I trust in God, they are gone, too! everything but the
Title:  water is still and at peace; in, then, where you may create those sounds you
Title:  love so well to hear.
Title:  
Title:  David smiled sadly, though not without a momentary gleam of pleasure, at
Title:  this allusion to his beloved vocation. He no longer hesitated to be led to a
Title:  spot which promised such unalloyed gratification to his wearied senses; and
Title:  leaning on the arm of his companion, he entered the narrow mouth of the
Title:  cave. Duncan seized a pile of the sassafras, which he drew before the
Title:  passage, studiously concealing every appearance of an aperture. Within this
Title:  fragile barrier he arranged the blankets abandoned by the foresters,
Title:  darkening the inner extremity of the cavern, while its outer received a
Title:  chastened light from the narrow ravine, through which one arm of the river
Title:  rushed to form the junction with its sister branch a few rods below.
Title:  
Title:  I like not the principle of the natives, which teaches them to submit
Title:  without a struggle, in emergencies that appear desperate, he said, while
Title:  busied in this employment; our own maxim, which says, while life remains
Title:  there is hope, is more consoling, and better suited to a soldier's
Title:  temperament. To you, Cora, I will urge no words of idle encouragement; your
Title:  own fortitude and undisturbed reason will teach you all that may become your
Title:  sex; but cannot we dry the tears of that trembling weeper on your bosom?
Title:  
Title:  I am calmer, Duncan, said Alice, raising herself from the arms of her
Title:  sister, and forcing an appearance of composure through her tears; much
Title:  calmer, now. Surely, in this hidden spot we are safe, we are secret, free
Title:  from injury; we will hope everything from those generous men who have risked
Title:  so much already in our behalf.
Title:  
Title:  Now does our gentle Alice speak like a daughter of Munro! said Heyward,
Title:  pausing to press her hand as he passed toward the outer entrance of the
Title:  cavern. With two such examples of courage before him, a man would be ashamed
Title:  to prove other than a hero. He then seated himself in the center of the
Title:  cavern, grasping his remaining pistol with a hand convulsively clenched,
Title:  while his contracted and frowning eye announced the sullen desperation of
Title:  his purpose. The Hurons, if they come, may not gain our position so easily
Title:  as they think, he slowly muttered; and propping his head back against the
Title:  rock, he seemed to await the result in patience, though his gaze was
Title:  unceasingly bent on the open avenue to their place of retreat.
Title:  
Title:  With the last sound of his voice, a deep, a long, and almost breathless
Title:  silence succeeded. The fresh air of the morning had penetrated the recess,
Title:  and its influence was gradually felt on the spirits of its inmates. As
Title:  minute after minute passed by, leaving them in undisturbed security, the
Title:  insinuating feeling of hope was gradually gaining possession of every bosom,
Title:  though each one felt reluctant to give utterance to expectations that the
Title:  next moment might so fearfully destroy.
Title:  
Title:  David alone formed an exception to these varying emotions. A gleam of light
Title:  from the opening crossed his wan countenance, and fell upon the pages of the
Title:  little volume, whose leaves he was again occupied in turning, as if
Title:  searching for some song more fitted to their condition than any that had yet
Title:  met their eye. He was, most probably, acting all this time under a confused
Title:  recollection of the promised consolation of Duncan. At length, it would
Title:  seem, his patient industry found its reward; for, without explanation or
Title:  apology, he pronounced aloud the words Isle of Wight, drew a long, sweet
Title:  sound from his pitch-pipe, and then ran through the preliminary modulations
Title:  of the air whose name he had just mentioned, with the sweeter tones of his
Title:  own musical voice.
Title:  
Title:  May not this prove dangerous? asked Cora, glancing her dark eye at Major
Title:  Heyward.
Title:  
Title:  Poor fellow! his voice is too feeble to be heard above the din of the falls,
Title:  was the answer; beside, the cavern will prove his friend. Let him indulge
Title:  his passions since it may be done without hazard.
Title:  
Title:  Isle of Wight! repeated David, looking about him with that dignity with
Title:  which he had long been wont to silence the whispering echoes of his school;
Title:  'tis a brave tune, and set to solemn words! let it be sung with meet
Title:  respect!
Title:  
Title:  After allowing a moment of stillness to enforce his discipline, the voice of
Title:  the singer was heard, in low, murmuring syllables, gradually stealing on the
Title:  ear, until it filled the narrow vault with sounds rendered trebly thrilling
Title:  by the feeble and tremulous utterance produced by his debility. The melody,
Title:  which no weakness could destroy, gradually wrought its sweet influence on
Title:  the senses of those who heard it. It even prevailed over the miserable
Title:  travesty of the song of David which the singer had selected from a volume of
Title:  similar effusions, and caused the sense to be forgotten in the insinuating
Title:  harmony of the sounds. Alice unconsciously dried her tears, and bent her
Title:  melting eyes on the pallid features of Gamut, with an expression of
Title:  chastened delight that she neither affected or wished to conceal. Cora
Title:  bestowed an approving smile on the pious efforts of the namesake of the
Title:  Jewish prince, and Heyward soon turned his steady, stern look from the
Title:  outlet of the cavern, to fasten it, with a milder character, on the face of
Title:  David, or to meet the wandering beams which at moments strayed from the
Title:  humid eyes of Alice. The open sympathy of the listeners stirred the spirit
Title:  of the votary of music, whose voice regained its richness and volume,
Title:  without losing that touching softness which proved its secret charm.
Title:  Exerting his renovated powers to their utmost, he was yet filling the arches
Title:  of the cave with long and full tones, when a yell burst into the air
Title:  without, that instantly stilled his pious strains, choking his voice
Title:  suddenly, as though his heart had literally bounded into the passage of his
Title:  throat.
Title:  
Title:  We are lost! exclaimed Alice, throwing herself into the arms of Cora.
Title:  
Title:  Not yet, not yet, returned the agitated but undaunted Heyward: the sound
Title:  came from the center of the island, and it has been produced by the sight of
Title:  their dead companions. We are not yet discovered, and there is still hope.
Title:  
Title:  Faint and almost despairing as was the prospect of escape, the words of
Title:  Duncan were not thrown away, for it awakened the powers of the sisters in
Title:  such a manner that they awaited the results in silence. A second yell soon
Title:  followed the first, when a rush of voices was heard pouring down the island,
Title:  from its upper to its lower extremity, until they reached the naked rock
Title:  above the caverns, where, after a shout of savage triumph, the air continued
Title:  full of horrible cries and screams, such as man alone can utter, and he only
Title:  when in a state of the fiercest barbarity.
Title:  
Title:  The sounds quickly spread around them in every direction. Some called to
Title:  their fellows from the water's edge, and were answered from the heights
Title:  above. Cries were heard in the startling vicinity of the chasm between the
Title:  two caves, which mingled with hoarser yells that arose out of the abyss of
Title:  the deep ravine. In short, so rapidly had the savage sounds diffused
Title:  themselves over the barren rock, that it was not difficult for the anxious
Title:  listeners to imagine they could be heard beneath, as in truth they were
Title:  above on every side of them.
Title:  
Title:  In the midst of this tumult, a triumphant yell was raised within a few yards
Title:  of the hidden entrance to the cave. Heyward abandoned every hope, with the
Title:  belief it was the signal that they were discovered. Again the impression
Title:  passed away, as he heard the voices collect near the spot where the white
Title:  man had so reluctantly abandoned his rifle. Amid the jargon of Indian
Title:  dialects that he now plainly heard, it was easy to distinguish not only
Title:  words, but sentences, in the patois of the Canadas. A burst of voices had
Title:  shouted simultaneously, La Longue Carabine! causing the oppostie woods to
Title:  re-echo with a name which, Heyward well remembered, had been given by his
Title:  enemies to a celebrated hunter and scout of the English camp, and who, he
Title:  now learned for the first time, had been his late companion.
Title:  
Title:  La Longue Carabine! La Longue Carabine! passed from mouth to mouth, until
Title:  the whole band appeared to be collected around a trophy which would seem to
Title:  announce the death of its formidable owner. After a vociferous consultation,
Title:  which was, at times, deafened by bursts of savage joy, they again separated,
Title:  filling the air with the name of a foe, whose body, Heywood could collect
Title:  from their expressions, they hoped to find concealed in some crevice of the
Title:  island.
Title:  
Title:  Now, he whispered to the trembling sisters, now is the moment of
Title:  uncertainty! if our place of retreat escape this scrutiny, we are still
Title:  safe! In every event, we are assured, by what has fallen from our enemies,
Title:  that our friends have escaped, and in two short hours we may look for succor
Title:  from Webb.
Title:  
Title:  There were now a few minutes of fearful stillness, during which Heyward well
Title:  knew that the savages conducted their search with greater vigilance and
Title:  method. More than once he could distinguish their footsteps, as they brushed
Title:  the sassafras, causing the faded leaves to rustle, and the branches to snap.
Title:  At length, the pile yielded a little, a corner of a blanket fell, and a
Title:  faint ray of light gleamed into the inner part of the cave. Cora folded
Title:  Alice to her bosom in agony, and Duncan sprang to his feet. A shout was at
Title:  that moment heard, as if issuing from the center of the rock, announcing
Title:  that the neighboring cavern had at length been entered. In a minute, the
Title:  number and loudness of the voices indicated that the whole party was
Title:  collected in and around that secret place.
Title:  
Title:  As the inner passages to the two caves were so close to each other, Duncan,
Title:  believing that escape was no longer possible, passed David and the sisters,
Title:  to place himself between the latter and the first onset of the terrible
Title:  meeting. Grown desperate by his situation, he drew nigh the slight barrier
Title:  which separated him only by a few feet from his relentless pursuers, and
Title:  placing his face to the casual opening, he even looked out with a sort of
Title:  desperate indifference, on their movements.
Title:  
Title:  Within reach of his arm was the brawny shoulder of a gigantic Indian, whose
Title:  deep and authoritative voice appeared to give directions to the proceedings
Title:  of his fellows. Beyond him again, Duncan could look into the vault opposite,
Title:  which was filled with savages, upturning and rifling the humble furniture of
Title:  the scout. The wound of David had dyed the leaves of sassafras with a color
Title:  that the native well knew as anticipating the season. Over this sign of
Title:  their success, they sent up a howl, like an opening from so many hounds who
Title:  had recovered a lost trail. After this yell of victory, they tore up the
Title:  fragrant bed of the cavern, and bore the branches into the chasm, scattering
Title:  the boughs, as if they suspected them of concealing the person of the man
Title:  they had so long hated and feared. One fierce and wild-looking warrior
Title:  approached the chief, bearing a load of the brush, and pointing exultingly
Title:  to the deep red stains with which it was sprinkled, uttered his joy in
Title:  Indian yells, whose meaning Heyward was only enabled to comprehend by the
Title:  frequent repetition of the name La Longue Carabine! When his triumph had
Title:  ceased, he cast the brush on the slight heap Duncan had made before the
Title:  entrance of the second cavern, and closed the view. His example was followed
Title:  by others, who, as they drew the branches from the cave of the scout, threw
Title:  them into one pile, adding, unconsciously, to the security of those they
Title:  sought. The very slightness of the defense was its chief merit, for no one
Title:  thought of disturbing a mass of brush, which all of them believed, in that
Title:  moment of hurry and confusion, had been accidentally raised by the hands of
Title:  their own party.
Title:  
Title:  As the blankets yielded before the outward pressure, and the branches
Title:  settled in the fissure of the rock by their own weight, forming a compact
Title:  body, Duncan once more breathed freely. With a light step and lighter heart,
Title:  he returned to the center of the cave, and took the place he had left, where
Title:  he could command a view of the opening next the river. While he was in the
Title:  act of making this movement, the Indians, as if changing their purpose by a
Title:  common impulse, broke away from the chasm in a body, and were heard rushing
Title:  up the island again, toward the point whence they had originally descended.
Title:  Here another wailing cry betrayed that they were again collected around the
Title:  bodies of their dead comrades.
Title:  
Title:  Duncan now ventured to look at his companions; for, during the most critical
Title:  moments of their danger, he had been apprehensive that the anxiety of his
Title:  countenance might communicate some additional alarm to those who were so
Title:  little able to sustain it.
Title:  
Title:  They are gone, Cora! he whispered; Alice, they are returned whence they
Title:  came, and we are saved! To Heaven, that has alone delivered us from the
Title:  grasp of so merciless an enemy, be all the praise!
Title:  
Title:  Then to Heaven will I return my thanks! exclaimed the younger sister, rising
Title:  from the encircling arm of Cora, and casting herself with enthusiastic
Title:  gratitude on the naked rock; to that Heaven who has spared the tears of a
Title:  gray-headed father; has saved the lives of those I so much love.
Title:  
Title:  Both Heyward and the more temperate Cora witnessed the act of involuntary
Title:  emotion with powerful sympathy, the former secretly believing that piety had
Title:  never worn a form so lovely as it had now assumed in the youthful person of
Title:  Alice. Her eyes were radiant with the glow of grateful feelings; the flush
Title:  of her beauty was again seated on her cheeks, and her whole soul seemed
Title:  ready and anxious to pour out its thanksgivings through the medium of her
Title:  eloquent features. But when her lips moved, the words they should have
Title:  uttered appeared frozen by some new and sudden chill. Her bloom gave place
Title:  to the paleness of death; her soft and melting eyes grew hard, and seemed
Title:  contracting with horror; while those hands, which she had raised, clasped in
Title:  each other, towardheaven, dropped in horizontal lines before her, the
Title:  fingers pointed forward in convulsed motion. Heyward turned the instant she
Title:  gave a direction to his suspicions, and peering just above the ledge which
Title:  formed the threshold of the open outlet of the cavern, he beheld the
Title:  malignant, fierce and savage features of Le Renard Subtil.
Title:  
Title:  In that moment of surprise, the self-possession of Heyward did not desert
Title:  him. He observed by the vacant expression of the Indian's countenance, that
Title:  his eye, accustomed to the open air had not yet been able to penetrate the
Title:  dusky light which pervaded the depth of the cavern. He had even thought of
Title:  retreating beyond a curvature in the natural wall, which might still conceal
Title:  him and his companions, when by the sudden gleam of intelligence that shot
Title:  across the features of the savage, he saw it was too late, and that they
Title:  were betrayed.
Title:  
Title:  The look of exultation and brutal triumph which announced this terrible
Title:  truth was irresistibly irritating. Forgetful of everything but the impulses
Title:  of his hot blood, Duncan levelled his pistol and fired. The report of the
Title:  weapon made the cavern bellow like an eruption from a volcano; and when the
Title:  smoke it vomited had been driven away before the current of air which issued
Title:  from the ravine the place so lately occupied by the features of his
Title:  treacherous guide was vacant. Rushing to the outlet, Heyward caught a
Title:  glimpse of his dark figure stealing around a low and narrow ledge, which
Title:  soon hid him entirely from sight.
Title:  
Title:  Among the savages a frightful stillness succeeded the explosion, which had
Title:  just been heard bursting from the bowels of the rock. But when Le Renard
Title:  raised his voice in a long and intelligible whoop, it was answered by a
Title:  spontaneous yell from the mouth of every Indian within hearing of the sound.
Title:  
Title:  The clamorous noises again rushed down the island; and before Duncan had
Title:  time to recover from the shock, his feeble barrier of brush was scattered to
Title:  the winds, the cavern was entered at both its extremities, and he and his
Title:  companions were dragged from their shelter and borne into the day, where
Title:  they stood surrounded by the whole band of the triumphant Hurons.
Title:  
Title:                 ----------------------------------------------
Title:  
Title:  Chapter 10
Title:  
Title:       I fear we shall outsleep the coming morn
Title:       As much as we this night have overwatched!
Title:  
Title:                                                 MIDSUMMER NIGHT'S DREAM
Title:  
Title:  The instant the shock of this sudden misfortune had abated, Duncan began to
Title:  make his observations on the appearance and proceedings of their captors.
Title:  Contrary to the usages of the natives in the wantonness of their success
Title:  they had respected, not only the persons of the trembling sisters, but his
Title:  own. The rich ornaments of his military attire had indeed been repeatedly
Title:  handled by different individuals of the tribes with eyes expressing a savage
Title:  longing to possess the baubles; but before the customary violence could be
Title:  resorted to, a mandate in the authoritative voice of the large warrior,
Title:  already mentioned, stayed the uplifted hand, and convinced Heyward that they
Title:  were to be reserved for some object of particular moment.
Title:  
Title:  While, however, these manifestations of weakness were exhibited by the young
Title:  and vain of the party, the more experienced warriors continued their search
Title:  throughout both caverns, with an activity that denoted they were far from
Title:  being satisfied with those fruits of their conquest which had already been
Title:  brought to light. Unable to discover any new victim, these diligent workers
Title:  of vengeance soon approached their male prisoners, pronouncing the name La
Title:  Longue Carabine, with a fierceness that could not be easily mistaken. Duncan
Title:  affected not to comprehend the meaning of their repeated and violent
Title:  interrogatories, while his companion was spared the effort of a similar
Title:  deception by his ignorance of French. Wearied at length by their
Title:  importunities, and apprehensive of irritating his captors by too stubborn a
Title:  silence, the former looked about him in quest of Magua, who might interpret
Title:  his answers to questions which were at each moment becoming more earnest and
Title:  threatening.
Title:  
Title:  The conduct of this savage had formed a solitary exception to that of all
Title:  his fellows. While the others were busily occupied in seeking to gratify
Title:  their childish passion for finery, by plundering even the miserable effects
Title:  of the scout, or had been searching with such bloodthirsty vengeance in
Title:  their looks for their absent owner, Le Renard had stood at a little distance
Title:  from the prisoners, with a demeanor so quiet and satisfied, as to betray
Title:  that he had already effected the grand purpose of his treachery. When the
Title:  eyes of Heyward first met those of his recent guide, he turned them away in
Title:  horror at the sinister though calm look he encountered. Conquering his
Title:  disgust, however, he was able, with an averted face, to address his
Title:  successful enemy.
Title:  
Title:  Le Renard Subtil is too much of a warrior, said the reluctant Heyward, to
Title:  refuse telling an unarmed man what his conquerors say.
Title:  
Title:  They ask for the hunter who knows the paths through the woods, returned
Title:  Magua, in his broken English, laying his hand, at the same time, with a
Title:  ferocious smile, on the bundle of leaves with which a wound on his own
Title:  shoulder was bandaged. La Longue Carabine'! his rifle is good, and his eye
Title:  never shut; but, like the short gun of the white chief, it is nothing
Title:  against the life of Le Subtil.
Title:  
Title:  Le Renard is too brave to remember the hurts received in war, or the hands
Title:  that gave them.
Title:  
Title:  Was it war, when the tired Indian rested at the sugartree to taste his corn!
Title:  who filled the bushes with creeping enemies! who drew the knife, whose
Title:  tongue was peace, while his heart was colored with blood! Did Magua say that
Title:  the hatchet was out of the ground, and that his hand had dug it up?
Title:  
Title:  As Duncan dared not retort upon his accuser by reminding him of his own
Title:  premeditated treachery, and disdained to deprecate his resentment by any
Title:  words of apology, he remained silent. Magua seemed also content to rest the
Title:  controversy as well as all further communication there, for he resumed the
Title:  leaning attitude against the rock from which, in momentary energy, he had
Title:  arisen. But the cry of La Longue Carabine was renewed the instant the
Title:  impatient savages perceived that the short dialogue was ended.
Title:  
Title:  You hear, said Magua, with stubborn indifference: the red Hurons call for
Title:  the life of The Long Rifle, or they will have the blood of him that keep him
Title:  hid!
Title:  
Title:  He is gone - escaped; he is far beyond their reach.
Title:  
Title:  Renard smiled with cold contempt, as he answered:
Title:  
Title:  When the white man dies, he thinks he is at peace; but the red men know how
Title:  to torture even the ghosts of their enemies. Where is his body? Let the
Title:  Hurons see his scalp.
Title:  
Title:  He is not dead, but escaped.
Title:  
Title:  Magua shook his head incredulously.
Title:  
Title:  Is he a bird, to spread his wings; or is he a fish, to swim without air! The
Title:  white chief read in his books, and he believes the Hurons are fools!
Title:  
Title:  Though no fish, The Long Rifle can swim. He floated down the stream when the
Title:  powder was all burned, and when the eyes of the Hurons were behind a cloud.
Title:  
Title:  And why did the white chief stay? demanded the still incredulous Indian. Is
Title:  he a stone that goes to the bottom, or does the scalp burn his head?
Title:  
Title:  That I am not stone, your dead comrade, who fell into the falls, might
Title:  answer, were the life still in him, said the provoked young man, using, in
Title:  his anger, that boastful language which was most likely to excite the
Title:  admiration of an Indian. The white man thinks none but cowards desert their
Title:  women.
Title:  
Title:  Magua muttered a few words, inaudibly, between his teeth, before he
Title:  continued, aloud:
Title:  
Title:  Can the Delawares swim, too, as well as crawl in the bushes? Where is Le
Title:  Gros Serpent?
Title:  
Title:  Duncan, who perceived by the use of these Canadian appellations, that his
Title:  late companions were much better known to his enemies than to himself,
Title:  answered, reluctantly: He also is gone down with the water.
Title:  
Title:  Le Cerf Agile is not here?
Title:  
Title:  I know not whom you call The Nimble Deer, said Duncan gladly profiting by
Title:  any excuse to create delay.
Title:  
Title:  Uncas, returned Magua, pronouncing the Delaware name with even greater
Title:  difficulty than he spoke his English words. Bounding Elk is what the white
Title:  man says, when he calls to the young Mohican.
Title:  
Title:  Here is some confusion in names between us, Le Renard, said Duncan, hoping
Title:  to provoke a discussion. Daim is the French for deer, and cerf for stag;
Title:  lan is the true term, when one would speak of an elk.
Title:  
Title:  Yes, muttered the Indian, in his native tongue; the pale faces are prattling
Title:  women! they have two words for each thing, while a red-skin will make the
Title:  sound of his voice speak to him. Then, changing his language, he continued,
Title:  adhering to the imperfect nomenclature of his provincial instructors. The
Title:  deer is swift, but weak; the elk is swift, but strong; and the son of Le
Title:  Serpent is Le Cerf Agile. Has he leaped the river to the woods?
Title:  
Title:  If you mean the younger Delaware, he, too, has gone down with the water.
Title:  
Title:  As there was nothing improbable to an Indian in the manner of the escape,
Title:  Magua admitted the truth of what he had heard, with a readiness that
Title:  afforded additional evidence how little he would prize such worthless
Title:  captives. With his companions, however, the feeling was manifestly
Title:  different.
Title:  
Title:  The Hurons had awaited the result of this short dialogue with characteristic
Title:  patience, and with a silence that increased until there was a general
Title:  stillness in the band. When Heyward ceased to speak, they turned their eyes,
Title:  as one man, on Magua, demanding, in this expressive manner, an explanation
Title:  of what had been said. Their interpreter pointed to the river, and made them
Title:  acquainted with the result, as much by the action as by the few words he
Title:  uttered. When the fact was generally understood, the savages raised a
